<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stinkdier.html>stinkdier</a> (14408)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stinken.html>stinken</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stink.html>stink</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dier.html>dier</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:animal.html>animal</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <a href = vnd.unilang:compare.html>Compare</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Stinktier</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:which.html>which</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> attested slightly earlier, <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">stinkdyr</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stinkdier.html>stinkdier</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stinkdieren.html>stinkdieren</a></b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:diminutive.html>diminutive</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stinkdiertje.html>stinkdiertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:skunk.html>skunk</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:any.html>any</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:member.html>member</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:family.html>family</a> Mephitidae <span class="defdate">[<a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> 1760s]</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stoer.html>stoer</a> (4346)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:originally.html>Originally</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:same.html>same</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:word.html>word</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:as.html>as</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stuurs.html>stuurs</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:which.html>which</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:it.html>it</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:an.html>an</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eastern.html>eastern</a> dialectal <a href = vnd.unilang:variant.html>variant</a>. Cognate <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">stur</i> (<a href = vnd.unilang:itself.html>itself</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:low.html>Low</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a>). <a href = vnd.unilang:not.html>Not</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:immediately.html>immediately</a> cognate <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language"><a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">stour</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">stor</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:but.html>but</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:possibly.html>possibly</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:related.html>related</a>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stofdoek.html>stofdoek</a> (112646)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stof.html>stof</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stoffen.html>stoffen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:doek.html>doek</a></i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stomp.html>stomp</a> (13437)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Cognate <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">stumpf</i>.
<span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:this.html>This</a> etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:missing.html>missing</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:incomplete.html>incomplete</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:please.html>Please</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:add.html>add</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:it.html>it</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:discuss.html>discuss</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:it.html>it</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:at.html>at</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
